#===============================================================================
#==TABLE no 4      : Ссылки документов
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock
T=1SCRDOC |Ссылки документов             |_1SCRDOC   |          
#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=ROW_ID                |Row ID              |I   |0     |0        
F=MDID                  |Md ID of select     |I   |0     |0        
F=PARENTVAL             |Parent Value        |C   |23    |0        
F=CHILD_DATE_TIME_IDDOC |Child date          |C   |23    |0        
F=CHILDID               |Child Doc ID        |C   |9     |0        
F=FLAGS                 |Flags of refers     |Y   |0     |0        
#----Indexes------
# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK__1SCRDOC                    |ROW_ID        |1     |ROW_ID                                                      |1          
I=CHILD                          |Child Referenc|1     |CHILDID,MDID,PARENTVAL                                      |0          
I=PARENT                         |Parent Referen|1     |MDID,PARENTVAL,CHILD_DATE_TIME_IDDOC                        |0          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp__1SCRDOC_Write           |              |@MdId I, @ParentVal C(23), @ChildDateTimeIdDoc C(23), @ChildId C(9), @Flags Y|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
UPDATE _1SCRDOC SET FLAGS=FLAGS|@Flags WHERE CHILDID=@ChildId AND MDID=@MdId AND PARENTVAL=@ParentVal
IF @@ROWCOUNT=0
    INSERT INTO _1SCRDOC VALUES ( @MdId, @ParentVal, @ChildDateTimeIdDoc, @ChildId, @Flags )
\}
#

#==PROCEDURE GetMaxID
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp__1SUIDCTL_GetMaxID       |GetMaxID      |@tid I, @id C(9) O                      |select @id=MAXID from _1SUIDCTL(NOLOCK) where TYPEID=@tid if @id is null select @id='         '
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE SetMaxID
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp__1SUIDCTL_SetMaxID       |SetMaxID      |@tid I, @id C(9) O                      |set nocount on declare @oid char(9) select @oid=MAXID from _1SUIDCTL where TYPEID=@tid if @oid is null insert into _1SUIDCTL values(@tid,@id) else begin if @oid<@id update _1SUIDCTL set MAXID=@id where TYPEID=@tid end
#

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod         |              |@BaseDate D, @Period C(1), @NewDate D O |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
SET DATEFIRST 1
DECLARE @Day int
IF @Period='D'
    SELECT @NewDate=@BaseDate

ELSE IF @Period='W'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, -DATEPART(dw, @BaseDate)+1, @BaseDate)

ELSE IF @Period='M'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(mm, DATEDIFF(mm, '1753-01-01', @BaseDate), '1753-01-01')

ELSE IF @Period='Q'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(qq, DATEDIFF(qq, '1753-01-01', @BaseDate), '1753-01-01')

ELSE IF @Period='Y'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(yy, DATEDIFF(yy, '1753-01-01', @BaseDate), '1753-01-01')

ELSE IF @Period='T'
    BEGIN
    SELECT @Day=DATEPART(dd, @BaseDate )
    IF @Day>15 SELECT @Day=15
    ELSE       SELECT @Day=0
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, @Day, DATEADD(mm, DATEDIFF(mm, '1753-01-01', @BaseDate), '1753-01-01'))
    END

ELSE IF @Period='C'
    BEGIN
    SELECT @Day=DATEPART(dd, @BaseDate )

    IF      @Day>20  SELECT @Day=20
    ELSE IF @Day>10  SELECT @Day=10
ELSE             SELECT @Day=0

        SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, @Day, DATEADD(mm, DATEDIFF(mm, '1753-01-01', @BaseDate), '1753-01-01'))
    END

ELSE IF @Period='F'
    BEGIN
        SELECT @Day=DATEPART(dd, @BaseDate )

        IF      @Day>25 SELECT @Day=25
        ELSE IF @Day>20 SELECT @Day=20
        ELSE IF @Day>15 SELECT @Day=15
        ELSE IF @Day>10 SELECT @Day=10
        ELSE IF @Day>5  SELECT @Day=5
        ELSE            SELECT @Day=0

        SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, @Day, DATEADD(mm, DATEDIFF(mm, '1753-01-01', @BaseDate), '1753-01-01'))
    END

ELSE SELECT @NewDate=CONVERT(datetime, '1753-01-01')
\}
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_GetNextPeriod            |              |@BaseDate D, @Period C(1), @NewDate D O |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
SET DATEFIRST 1
DECLARE @BeginOfPeriod datetime
DECLARE @day integer
EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @BaseDate, @Period, @BeginOfPeriod OUTPUT

IF @Period='D'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, 1,  @BeginOfPeriod)
ELSE IF @Period='W'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(wk, 1,  @BeginOfPeriod)
ELSE IF @Period='M'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(mm, 1,  @BeginOfPeriod)
ELSE IF @Period='Q'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(qq, 1,  @BeginOfPeriod)
ELSE IF @Period='Y'
    SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(yy, 1,  @BeginOfPeriod)
ELSE IF @Period='T' BEGIN
    SELECT @day=DATEPART(dd, @BeginOfPeriod)
    IF @day>15 SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(mm, DATEDIFF(mm, '1753-01-01', @BeginOfPeriod), '1753-02-01')
    ELSE       SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, 15, @BeginOfPeriod)
END
ELSE IF @Period='C' BEGIN
    SELECT @day=DATEPART(dd, @BeginOfPeriod)
    IF @day>20 SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(mm, DATEDIFF(mm, '1753-01-01', @BeginOfPeriod), '1753-02-01')
    ELSE       SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, 10, @BeginOfPeriod)
END
ELSE IF @Period='F' BEGIN
    SELECT @day=DATEPART(dd, @BeginOfPeriod)
    IF @day>25 SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(mm, DATEDIFF(mm, '1753-01-01', @BeginOfPeriod), '1753-02-01')
    ELSE       SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, 5,  @BeginOfPeriod)
END
ELSE SELECT @NewDate=CONVERT(datetime, '1753-01-01')
\}
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_GetEndOfPeriod           |              |@BaseDate D, @Period C(1), @NewDate D O |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @NextPeriod  datetime

EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @BaseDate, @Period, @NextPeriod OUTPUT
SELECT @NewDate=DATEADD(dd, -1,  @NextPeriod)
\}
#

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH3957_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum1 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum2 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum3 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum4 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP3948),0),@Sum1=COALESCE(SUM(SP3951),0),@Sum2=COALESCE(SUM(SP3952),0),@Sum3=COALESCE(SUM(SP3953),0),@Sum4=COALESCE(SUM(SP3954),0) FROM DT3957 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
    IF ABS(@Sum2)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum2=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum2)
    IF ABS(@Sum3)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum3=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum3)
    IF ABS(@Sum4)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum4=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum4)
UPDATE DH3957 SET SP3948=@Sum0,SP3951=@Sum1,SP3952=@Sum2,SP3953=@Sum3,SP3954=@Sum4 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

#
#===============================================================================
#==TABLE no 83     : Документ (Мн.ч.) ИнвентаризацияТМЦ
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock
T=DT3725  |Документ (Мн.ч.) Инвентаризаци|DT3725     |          
#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=IDDOC                 |ID Document's       |C   |9     |0        
F=LINENO_               |LineNo              |S   |0     |0        
F=SP3716                |(P)Номенклатура     |C   |9     |0        
F=SP3717                |(P)Количество       |N   |13    |3        
F=SP3718                |(P)КоличествоУчет   |N   |13    |3        
F=SP3719                |(P)Единица          |C   |9     |0        
F=SP3720                |(P)Коэффициент      |N   |9     |3        
F=SP3721                |(P)Цена             |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3722                |(P)Сумма            |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3723                |(P)СуммаУчет        |N   |14    |2        
#----Indexes------
# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_DT3725                      |of IDDOC+LineN|1     |IDDOC,LINENO_                                               |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH3725_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum1 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP3722),0),@Sum1=COALESCE(SUM(SP3723),0) FROM DT3725 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
UPDATE DH3725 SET SP3722=@Sum0,SP3723=@Sum1 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

#===============================================================================
#==TABLE no 96     : Документ (Мн.ч.) ОтчетККМ
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock
T=DT3114  |Документ (Мн.ч.) ОтчетККМ     |DT3114     |          
#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=IDDOC                 |ID Document's       |C   |9     |0

F=SP3102                |(P)Номенклатура     |C   |9     |0

F=SP3104                |(P)Единица          |C   |9     |0        
F=SP3105                |(P)Коэффициент      |N   |9     |3        
F=SP3106                |(P)Цена             |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3107                |(P)Сумма            |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3108                |(P)СтавкаНДС        |C   |9     |0        
F=SP3109                |(P)СуммаНДС         |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3110                |(P)СтавкаНП         |C   |9     |0        
F=SP3111                |(P)СуммаНП          |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3112                |(P)Партия           |C   |9     |0

# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_DT3114                      |of IDDOC+LineN|1     |IDDOC,LINENO_                                               |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH3114_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum1 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum2 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP3107),0),@Sum1=COALESCE(SUM(SP3109),0),@Sum2=COALESCE(SUM(SP3111),0) FROM DT3114 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
    IF ABS(@Sum2)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum2=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum2)
UPDATE DH3114 SET SP3107=@Sum0,SP3109=@Sum1,SP3111=@Sum2 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

F=SP3915                |(P)СуммаНДС         |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3916                |(P)СтавкаНП         |C   |9     |0        
F=SP3917                |(P)СуммаНП          |N   |14    |2        
F=SP1626                |(P)Партия           |C   |9     |0        
#----Indexes------
# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_DT1628                      |of IDDOC+LineN|1     |IDDOC,LINENO_                                               |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH1628_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum1 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum2 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP1625),0),@Sum1=COALESCE(SUM(SP3915),0),@Sum2=COALESCE(SUM(SP3917),0) FROM DT1628 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
    IF ABS(@Sum2)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum2=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum2)
UPDATE DH1628 SET SP1625=@Sum0,SP3915=@Sum1,SP3917=@Sum2 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock

# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=IDDOC                 |ID Document's       |C   |9     |0

F=SP1782                |(P)Номенклатура     |C   |9     |0

F=SP1784                |(P)Единица          |C   |9     |0        
F=SP1785                |(P)Коэффициент      |N   |9     |3

#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH1790_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP1787),0) FROM DT1790 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
UPDATE DH1790 SET SP1787=@Sum0 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
    IF ABS(@Sum2)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum2=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum2)
UPDATE DH3089 SET SP3086=@Sum0,SP4183=@Sum1,SP4185=@Sum2 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH2988_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum1 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum2 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP2983),0),@Sum1=COALESCE(SUM(SP2985),0),@Sum2=COALESCE(SUM(SP3688),0) FROM DT2988 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
    IF ABS(@Sum2)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum2=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum2)
UPDATE DH2988 SET SP2983=@Sum0,SP2985=@Sum1,SP3688=@Sum2 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc

#==TABLE no 147    : Документ (Мн.ч.) ЧекККМ
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock

#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=IDDOC                 |ID Document's       |C   |9     |0

F=SP3038                |(P)ШтрихКод         |C   |13    |0

F=SP3040                |(P)Количество       |N   |13    |3        
F=SP3041                |(P)Единица          |C   |9     |0        
F=SP3042                |(P)Коэффициент      |N   |9     |3

F=SP3044                |(P)Сумма            |N   |14    |2

# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_DT3046                      |of IDDOC+LineN|1     |IDDOC,LINENO_                                               |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH3046_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP3044),0) FROM DT3046 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
UPDATE DH3046 SET SP3044=@Sum0 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH9017_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum1 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum2 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum3 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum4 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum5 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum6 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum7 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP9005),0),@Sum1=COALESCE(SUM(SP9006),0),@Sum2=COALESCE(SUM(SP9010),0),@Sum3=COALESCE(SUM(SP9011),0),@Sum4=COALESCE(SUM(SP9012),0),@Sum5=COALESCE(SUM(SP9013),0),@Sum6=COALESCE(SUM(SP9014),0),@Sum7=COALESCE(SUM(SP9015),0) FROM DT9017 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
    IF ABS(@Sum2)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum2=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum2)
    IF ABS(@Sum3)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum3=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum3)
    IF ABS(@Sum4)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum4=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum4)
    IF ABS(@Sum5)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum5=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum5)
    IF ABS(@Sum6)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum6=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum6)
    IF ABS(@Sum7)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum7=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum7)
UPDATE DH9017 SET SP9005=@Sum0,SP9006=@Sum1,SP9010=@Sum2,SP9011=@Sum3,SP9012=@Sum4,SP9013=@Sum5,SP9014=@Sum6,SP9015=@Sum7 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_DH9133_UpdateTotals      |              |@IdDoc C(9)                             |{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @Sum0 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum1 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum2 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum3 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum4 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum5 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum6 NUMERIC(28,2),@Sum7 NUMERIC(28,2) 
SELECT @Sum0=COALESCE(SUM(SP9120),0),@Sum1=COALESCE(SUM(SP9121),0),@Sum2=COALESCE(SUM(SP9125),0),@Sum3=COALESCE(SUM(SP9126),0),@Sum4=COALESCE(SUM(SP9127),0),@Sum5=COALESCE(SUM(SP9128),0),@Sum6=COALESCE(SUM(SP9129),0),@Sum7=COALESCE(SUM(SP9130),0) FROM DT9133 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
    IF ABS(@Sum0)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum0=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum0)
    IF ABS(@Sum1)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum1=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum1)
    IF ABS(@Sum2)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum2=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum2)
    IF ABS(@Sum3)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum3=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum3)
    IF ABS(@Sum4)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum4=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum4)
    IF ABS(@Sum5)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum5=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum5)
    IF ABS(@Sum6)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum6=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum6)
    IF ABS(@Sum7)>999999999999.99 SELECT @Sum7=999999999999.99*SIGN(@Sum7)
UPDATE DH9133 SET SP9120=@Sum0,SP9121=@Sum1,SP9125=@Sum2,SP9126=@Sum3,SP9127=@Sum4,SP9128=@Sum5,SP9129=@Sum6,SP9130=@Sum7 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
\}

# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG639_Change             |              |@per D,@p1 C(9),@p2 C(9),@p3 N(14,2),@p4 N(14,2),@p5 N(14,2)|{\
Set Nocount On
Update RG639
  set SP644=Case When ABS(SP644+@p3)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP644+@p3 End,SP642=Case When ABS(SP642+@p4)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP642+@p4 End,SP643=Case When ABS(SP643+@p5)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP643+@p5 End
  where PERIOD=@per AND SP4066=@p1 AND SP641=@p2
if @@ROWCOUNT=0
    insert into RG639 values(@per,@p1,@p2,@p3,@p4,@p5)
\}

#===============================================================================
#==TABLE no 157    : Регистр (Дв.) Банк
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock
T=RA639   |Регистр (Дв.) Банк            |RA639      |          
#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=IDDOC                 |ID Document's       |C   |9     |0        
F=LINENO_               |LineNo              |S   |0     |0        
F=ACTNO                 |Action No           |I   |0     |0        
F=DEBKRED               |Flag Debet/Kredit   |L   |0     |0        
F=SP4066                |(P)Фирма            |C   |9     |0        
F=SP641                 |(P)БанковскийСчет   |C   |9     |0        
F=SP644                 |(P)СуммаВал         |N   |14    |2

# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_RA639                       |of IDDOC+LineN|1     |IDDOC,LINENO_,ACTNO                                         |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA639_ClearRecalcDocActs |              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA639 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4066, SP641, SP644, SP642, SP643  FROM RA639 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA639
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA639 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG639_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG639_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG639_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA639 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
END
CLOSE Cur_RA639
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA639
\}
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA639_WriteDocAct        |              |@IdDoc C(9), @LineNo S, @ActNo I, @DebetCredit L, @p0 C(9), @p1 C(9), @f0 N(14,2), @f1 N(14,2), @f2 N(14,2), @g0 C(9), @g1 C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM

EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @PeriodTA, @SnapShotPeriod, @PeriodTA OUTPUT
INSERT INTO RA639 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2, @g0, @g1)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG639_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
    END
END
ELSE
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG639_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG639_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @f0, @f1, @f2
END
\}

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA464_WriteDocAct        |              |@IdDoc C(9), @LineNo S, @ActNo I, @DebetCredit L, @p0 C(9), @p1 C(9), @p2 C(9), @p3 C(9), @f0 N(14,5), @f1 N(14,2), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I|{\

DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM

EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @PeriodTA, @SnapShotPeriod, @PeriodTA OUTPUT
INSERT INTO RA464 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG464_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
    END
END
ELSE
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG464_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1
IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG464_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1
END

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG4667_Change            |              |@per D,@p1 C(9),@p2 C(9),@p3 C(9),@p4 N(14,5)|{\
Set Nocount On
Update RG4667
  set SP4666=Case When ABS(SP4666+@p4)>999999999.99999 Then 999999999.99999 Else SP4666+@p4 End
  where PERIOD=@per AND SP4663=@p1 AND SP4664=@p2 AND SP4665=@p3
if @@ROWCOUNT=0
    insert into RG4667 values(@per,@p1,@p2,@p3,@p4)
\}

#-----Fields-------

F=IDDOC                 |ID Document's       |C   |9     |0

#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4667_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 5)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA4667 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4663, SP4664, SP4665, SP4666  FROM RA4667 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA4667
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4667 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG4667_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4667_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4667_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4667 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0
END
CLOSE Cur_RA4667
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA4667
\}
#

SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM

EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @PeriodTA, @SnapShotPeriod, @PeriodTA OUTPUT
INSERT INTO RA635 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2, @g0, @g1)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG635_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
    END
END
ELSE
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG635_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG635_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
END
\}

P=_1sp_RG3549_TLockX            |EscalateTLockX|                                        |set nocount on declare @i integer select @i=1 from RG3549(TABLOCKX HOLDLOCK) where 0=1
#
#===============================================================================
#==TABLE no 166    : Регистр КнигаПокупок
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock
T=RG3549  |Регистр КнигаПокупок          |RG3549     |          
#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=PERIOD                |Period Registr      |D   |0     |0        
F=SP4315                |(P)КредДокумент     |C   |13    |0        
F=SP4316                |(P)СтавкаНДС        |C   |9     |0        
F=SP4317                |(P)ВидДолга         |C   |9     |0        
F=SP4318                |(P)СуммаРуб         |N   |14    |2        
F=SP3546                |(P)СуммаНДС         |N   |14    |2        
F=SP4319                |(P)СуммаНП          |N   |14    |2        
#----Indexes------
# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_RG3549                      |PERIOD+PROP   |1     |PERIOD,SP4315,SP4316,SP4317                                 |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG3549_Change            |              |@per D,@p1 C(13),@p2 C(9),@p3 C(9),@p4 N(14,2),@p5 N(14,2),@p6 N(14,2)|{\
Set Nocount On
Update RG3549
  set SP4318=Case When ABS(SP4318+@p4)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP4318+@p4 End,SP3546=Case When ABS(SP3546+@p5)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP3546+@p5 End,SP4319=Case When ABS(SP4319+@p6)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP4319+@p6 End
  where PERIOD=@per AND SP4315=@p1 AND SP4316=@p2 AND SP4317=@p3
if @@ROWCOUNT=0
    insert into RG3549 values(@per,@p1,@p2,@p3,@p4,@p5,@p6)
\}
#

# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source

#

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA3549_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(13), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA3549 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4315, SP4316, SP4317, SP4318, SP3546, SP4319  FROM RA3549 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA3549
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA3549 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG3549_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG3549_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG3549_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA3549 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
END
CLOSE Cur_RA3549
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA3549
\}
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source

IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG3549_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2

    EXECUTE _1sp_RG3549_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4343_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(13), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA4343 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4336, SP4337, SP4365, SP4338, SP4339, SP4340  FROM RA4343 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA4343
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4343 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG4343_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4343_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4343_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4343 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @f0, @f1, @f2
END
CLOSE Cur_RA4343
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA4343
\}

#----Indexes------
# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_RA405                       |of IDDOC+LineN|1     |IDDOC,LINENO_,ACTNO                                         |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA405_ClearRecalcDocActs |              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 5)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA405 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4062, SP408, SP418, SP3117, SP411  FROM RA405 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA405
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA405 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG405_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG405_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG405_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA405 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0
END
CLOSE Cur_RA405
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA405
\}

# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source

INSERT INTO RA405 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @g0)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG405_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0

    END

    EXECUTE _1sp_RG405_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0

    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG405_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0
END
\}

  where PERIOD=@per AND SP4061=@p1 AND SP330=@p2 AND SP331=@p3 AND SP340=@p4 AND SP341=@p5 AND SP1554=@p6 AND SP7404=@p7

    insert into RG328 values(@per,@p1,@p2,@p3,@p4,@p5,@p6,@p7,@p8,@p9,@p10,@p11,@p12)

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA328_ClearRecalcDocActs |              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(9), @p4 CHAR(9), @p5 DATETIME, @p6 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 5), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f3 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f4 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA328 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4061, SP330, SP331, SP340, SP341, SP1554, SP7404, SP342, SP421, SP343, SP344, SP8855  FROM RA328 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA328
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA328 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3, @f4=-@f4
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG328_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG328_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG328_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA328 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4
END
CLOSE Cur_RA328
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA328
\}
#

# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source

    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3, @f4=-@f4

    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG328_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
    END
END
ELSE
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG328_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4
IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG328_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA351_ClearRecalcDocActs |              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(9), @p4 CHAR(9), @p5 CHAR(13), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 5), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f3 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f4 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f5 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA351 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4063, SP365, SP354, SP355, SP356, SP364, SP357, SP422, SP423, SP746, SP3539, SP8856  FROM RA351 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA351
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA351 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3, @f4=-@f4, @f5=-@f5
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG351_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG351_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG351_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA351 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
END
CLOSE Cur_RA351
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA351
\}

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA351_WriteDocAct        |              |@IdDoc C(9), @LineNo S, @ActNo I, @DebetCredit L, @p0 C(9), @p1 C(9), @p2 C(9), @p3 C(9), @p4 C(9), @p5 C(13), @f0 N(14,5), @f1 N(14,2), @f2 N(14,2), @f3 N(14,2), @f4 N(14,2), @f5 N(14,2), @g0 C(9), @g1 N(14,2), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM

EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @PeriodTA, @SnapShotPeriod, @PeriodTA OUTPUT
INSERT INTO RA351 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5, @g0, @g1)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3, @f4=-@f4, @f5=-@f5
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG351_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
    END
END
ELSE
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG351_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG351_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
END

#==TABLE no 176    : Регистр ПодотчетныеЛица

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG2964_Change            |              |@per D,@p1 C(9),@p2 C(9),@p3 C(9),@p4 C(13),@p5 N(14,2),@p6 N(14,2),@p7 N(14,2)|{\
Set Nocount On
Update RG2964
  set SP2960=Case When ABS(SP2960+@p5)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP2960+@p5 End,SP2961=Case When ABS(SP2961+@p6)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP2961+@p6 End,SP2962=Case When ABS(SP2962+@p7)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP2962+@p7 End
  where PERIOD=@per AND SP4068=@p1 AND SP3000=@p2 AND SP3001=@p3 AND SP2959=@p4
if @@ROWCOUNT=0
    insert into RG2964 values(@per,@p1,@p2,@p3,@p4,@p5,@p6,@p7)
\}

#==TABLE no 177    : Регистр (Дв.) ПодотчетныеЛица

# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA2964_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(13), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA2964 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4068, SP3000, SP3001, SP2959, SP2960, SP2961, SP2962  FROM RA2964 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA2964
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA2964 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG2964_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG2964_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG2964_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA2964 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2
END
CLOSE Cur_RA2964
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA2964
\}
#

INSERT INTO RA2964 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @g0)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4335_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(9), @p4 CHAR(13), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f3 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f4 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f5 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA4335 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4322, SP4323, SP4324, SP4325, SP4326, SP4327, SP4328, SP4329, SP4330, SP4331, SP8792  FROM RA4335 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA4335
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4335 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3, @f4=-@f4, @f5=-@f5
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG4335_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4335_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4335_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4335 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
END
CLOSE Cur_RA4335
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA4335
\}

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG4314_Change            |              |@per D,@p1 C(9),@p2 C(9),@p3 C(9),@p4 C(13),@p5 N(14,2),@p6 N(14,2),@p7 N(14,2),@p8 N(14,2)|{\

Update RG4314
  set SP4309=Case When ABS(SP4309+@p5)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP4309+@p5 End,SP4310=Case When ABS(SP4310+@p6)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP4310+@p6 End,SP4311=Case When ABS(SP4311+@p7)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP4311+@p7 End,SP8793=Case When ABS(SP8793+@p8)>999999999999.99 Then 999999999999.99 Else SP8793+@p8 End
  where PERIOD=@per AND SP4305=@p1 AND SP4306=@p2 AND SP4307=@p3 AND SP4308=@p4
if @@ROWCOUNT=0
    insert into RG4314 values(@per,@p1,@p2,@p3,@p4,@p5,@p6,@p7,@p8)
\}

#==TABLE no 181    : Регистр (Дв.) Поставщики
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock
T=RA4314  |Регистр (Дв.) Поставщики      |RA4314     |          
#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=IDDOC                 |ID Document's       |C   |9     |0

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4314_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(13), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f3 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA4314 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4305, SP4306, SP4307, SP4308, SP4309, SP4310, SP4311, SP8793  FROM RA4314 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA4314
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4314 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG4314_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4314_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4314_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4314 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
END
CLOSE Cur_RA4314
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA4314
\}
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4314_WriteDocAct       |              |@IdDoc C(9), @LineNo S, @ActNo I, @DebetCredit L, @p0 C(9), @p1 C(9), @p2 C(9), @p3 C(13), @f0 N(14,2), @f1 N(14,2), @f2 N(14,2), @f3 N(14,2), @g0 C(9), @g1 C(13), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM

EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @PeriodTA, @SnapShotPeriod, @PeriodTA OUTPUT
INSERT INTO RA4314 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @g0, @g1)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4314_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
    END
END
ELSE
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG4314_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG4314_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3
END
\}

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA2351_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(9), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f2 NUMERIC(14, 5), @f3 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f4 NUMERIC(14, 2), @f5 NUMERIC(14, 5)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA2351 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP2343, SP2344, SP2345, SP4067, SP2349, SP2350, SP2375, SP5191, SP5192, SP5193  FROM RA2351 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA2351
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA2351 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1, @f2=-@f2, @f3=-@f3, @f4=-@f4, @f5=-@f5
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG2351_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG2351_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG2351_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA2351 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @f0, @f1, @f2, @f3, @f4, @f5
END
CLOSE Cur_RA2351
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA2351
\}

F=SP439                 |(P)Договор          |C   |9     |0        
F=SP441                 |(P)Номенклатура     |C   |9     |0        
F=SP445                 |(P)Партия           |C   |9     |0        
F=SP2833                |(P)ДокПродажи       |C   |13    |0        
F=SP442                 |(P)Количество       |N   |14    |5        
F=SP443                 |(P)ПродСтоимость    |N   |14    |2        
F=SP5063                |(P)Вознаграждение   |N   |14    |2        
#----Indexes------
# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_RA438                       |of IDDOC+LineN|1     |IDDOC,LINENO_,ACTNO                                         |1          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA438_ClearRecalcDocActs |              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(9), @p4 CHAR(13), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 5), @f1 NUMERIC(14, 2)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA438 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4064, SP439, SP441, SP445, SP2833, SP442, SP443  FROM RA438 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA438
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA438 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG438_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG438_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG438_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA438 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
END
CLOSE Cur_RA438
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA438
\}
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA438_WriteDocAct        |              |@IdDoc C(9), @LineNo S, @ActNo I, @DebetCredit L, @p0 C(9), @p1 C(9), @p2 C(9), @p3 C(9), @p4 C(13), @f0 N(14,5), @f1 N(14,2), @g0 N(14,2), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON

EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @PeriodTA, @SnapShotPeriod, @PeriodTA OUTPUT
INSERT INTO RA438 VALUES(@IdDoc, @LineNo, @ActNo, @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1, @g0)
IF @DebetCredit=1
    SELECT @f0=-@f0, @f1=-@f1
IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
    SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
    WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG438_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
    END
END
ELSE
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG438_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
    EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
    EXECUTE _1sp_RG438_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0, @f1
END
\}

#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE EscalateTLock
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG4480_TLock             |EscalateTLock |                                        |set nocount on declare @i integer select @i=1 from RG4480(TABLOCK HOLDLOCK) where 0=1
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE EscalateTLockX
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG4480_TLockX            |EscalateTLockX|                                        |set nocount on declare @i integer select @i=1 from RG4480(TABLOCKX HOLDLOCK) where 0=1
#
#===============================================================================
#==TABLE no 186    : Регистр РезервыТМЦ
# Name    |Descr                         |SQLTableNam|RecordLock
T=RG4480  |Регистр РезервыТМЦ            |RG4480     |          
#-----Fields-------
# Name                  |Descr               |Type|Length|Precision
F=PERIOD                |Period Registr      |D   |0     |0        
F=SP4475                |(P)Фирма            |C   |9     |0        
F=SP4477                |(P)Номенклатура     |C   |9     |0        
F=SP4476                |(P)Склад            |C   |9     |0        
F=SP4519                |(P)ДоговорПокупателя|C   |9     |0        
F=SP4762                |(P)ЗаявкаПокупателя |C   |9     |0        
F=SP4479                |(P)Количество       |N   |14    |5        
#----Indexes------
# Name                           |Descr         |Unique|Indexed fields                                              |Type       
I=PK_RG4480                      |PERIOD+PROP   |1     |PERIOD,SP4475,SP4477,SP4476,SP4519,SP4762                   |1          
I=VIA4477                        |VIA4477       |0     |PERIOD,SP4477                                               |0          
I=VIA4762                        |VIA4762       |0     |PERIOD,SP4762                                               |0          
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG4480_Change            |              |@per D,@p1 C(9),@p2 C(9),@p3 C(9),@p4 C(9),@p5 C(9),@p6 N(14,5)|{\
Set Nocount On
Update RG4480
  set SP4479=Case When ABS(SP4479+@p6)>999999999.99999 Then 999999999.99999 Else SP4479+@p6 End
  where PERIOD=@per AND SP4475=@p1 AND SP4477=@p2 AND SP4476=@p3 AND SP4519=@p4 AND SP4762=@p5
if @@ROWCOUNT=0
    insert into RG4480 values(@per,@p1,@p2,@p3,@p4,@p5,@p6)
\}
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RG4480_Select            |              |@per D,@p1 C(9),@p2 C(9),@p3 C(9),@p4 C(9),@p5 C(9),@p6 N(14,5) O|Select @p6=SP4479 from RG4480 where PERIOD=@per AND SP4475=@p1 AND SP4477=@p2 AND SP4476=@p3 AND SP4519=@p4 AND SP4762=@p5
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE EscalateTLock
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4480_TLock             |EscalateTLock |                                        |set nocount on declare @i integer select @i=1 from RA4480(TABLOCK HOLDLOCK) where 0=1
#
#===============================================================================
#==PROCEDURE EscalateTLockX
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4480_TLockX            |EscalateTLockX|                                        |set nocount on declare @i integer select @i=1 from RA4480(TABLOCKX HOLDLOCK) where 0=1
#

#==PROCEDURE 
# Name                          |Descr         |Parameters                              |Source                                                                          
P=_1sp_RA4480_ClearRecalcDocActs|              |@IdDoc C(9), @DocDate D, @CurPeriod D, @RepeatToTM I, @SaveTurnsWithMonth I, @Direct I|{\
SET NOCOUNT ON
DECLARE @PeriodTA datetime, @Period datetime, @SnapShotPeriod char, @DebetCredit BIT
DECLARE @p0 CHAR(9), @p1 CHAR(9), @p2 CHAR(9), @p3 CHAR(9), @p4 CHAR(9), @f0 NUMERIC(14, 5)
SELECT @PeriodTA=CURDATE, @SnapShotPeriod=SNAPSHPER FROM _1SSYSTEM
DECLARE Cur_RA4480 CURSOR FOR SELECT DEBKRED, SP4475, SP4477, SP4476, SP4519, SP4762, SP4479  FROM RA4480 WHERE IDDOC=@IdDoc
OPEN Cur_RA4480
FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4480 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0
WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN

    IF @DebetCredit<>@Direct
        SELECT @f0=-@f0
    IF @RepeatToTM=1 BEGIN
        SELECT @Period=@CurPeriod
        WHILE @Period<=@PeriodTA BEGIN
            EXECUTE _1sp_RG4480_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0
            EXECUTE _1sp_GetNextPeriod @Period, @SnapShotPeriod, @Period OUTPUT
        END
    END
    ELSE
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4480_Change @CurPeriod, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0
    IF @SaveTurnsWithMonth=1 BEGIN
        EXECUTE _1sp_GetBeginOfPeriod @DocDate, 'M', @Period OUTPUT
        EXECUTE _1sp_RG4480_Change @Period, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0
    END

    FETCH NEXT FROM Cur_RA4480 INTO @DebetCredit, @p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @f0
END
CLOSE Cur_RA4480
DEALLOCATE Cur_RA4480
\}
